1);\\n            var dayPeriodLen = extraLength < 2 ? 1 : 3 + (extraLength >> 1);\\n            var dayPeriodChar = 'a';\\n            var hourChar = getDefaultHourSymbolFromLocale(locale);\\n locale.hourCycles &&\\n        // @ts-ignore\\n        locale.hourCycles.length) {\\n        // @ts-ignore\\n        hourCycle = locale.hourCycles[0];\\n    }\\n    if (hourCycle) {\\n        switch
